  <l xml:id="SS.4.9.36"><label>ci.9.36</label> tridroṇe 'pāṃ pacedyāvat ṣaṭprasthaṃ
  pariśeṣitam | śakṛdrasadadhikṣīramūtrāṇāṃ pṛthagāḍhakam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.9.37"><label>ci.9.37</label> tadvadghṛtasya tatsādhyaṃ
  bhūnimbavyoṣacitrakaiḥ | karañjaphalanīlikāśyāmāvalgujapīlubhiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.9.38"><label>ci.9.38</label> nīlinīnimbakusumaiḥ siddhaṃ
  kuṣṭhāpahaṃ ghṛtam | mrakṣaṇādaṅgasāvarṇyaṃ śvitriṇāṃ janayennṛṇām |
  bhagandaraṃ kṛmīnarśo mahānīlaṃ niyacchati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.9.39"><label>ci.9.39</label> mūtraṃ gavyaṃ citrakavyoṣayuktaṃ
  sarpiḥkumbhe kṣaudrayuktaṃ sthitaṃ hi | pakṣādūrdhvaṃ śvitribhiḥ peyametat
  kuryāc cāsmin kuṣṭhadiṣṭaṃ vidhānam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.9.40"><label>ci.9.40</label> pūtīkārkasruṅnarendradrumāṇāṃ
  mūtraiḥ piṣṭāḥ pallavāḥ saumanāś ca | lepaḥ śvitraṃ hanti dadrūrvraṇāṃś ca
  duṣṭānyarśāṃsyeṣa pāṭhā 'guruharidrākaṣāyaṃ,
  piṣṭamehinaṃ haridrādāruharidrākaṣāyaṃ, sāndramehinaṃ saptaparṇakaṣāyaṃ,
  śukramehinaṃ dūrvāśaivalaplavahaṭhakarañjakaserukakaṣāyaṃ
  kakubhacandanakaṣāyaṃ vā, phenamehinaṃ triphalāragvaghamṛdvīkākaṣāyaṃ,
  madhumadhuramiti; paittikeṣu nīlamehinaṃ śālasārādikaṣāyamaśvatthakaṣāyaṃ vā
  pāyayet, haridrāmehinaṃ rājavṛkṣakaṣāyaṃ, amlamehinaṃ nyagrodhādikaṣāyaṃ,
  kṣāramehinaṃ triphalākaṣāyaṃ, mañjiṣṭhāmehinaṃ mañjiṣṭhācandanakaṣāyaṃ,
  śoṇitamehinaṃ guḍūcītindukāsthikāśmaryakharjūrakaṣāyaṃ madhumiśraṃ; ata
  ūrdhvamasādhyeṣv api yogān yāpanārthaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ, tadyathā sarpirmehinaṃ
  kuṣṭhakuṭajapāṭhāhiṅgukaṭurohiṇīkalkaṃ guḍūcīcitrakakaṣāyeṇa pāyayet,
  vasāmehinamagnimanthakaṣāyaṃ śiṃśapākaṣāyaṃ vā, kṣaudramehinaṃ
  kadarakramukakaṣāyaṃ,
  hastimehinaṃ tindukakapitthaśirīṣapalāśapāṭhāmūrvāduḥsthikṣāraṃ ceti;
  dahyamānamaudakakandakvāthasiddhāṃ yavāgūṃ kṣīrekṣurasamadhurāṃ pāyayet || </l>


  <l xml:id="SS.4.11.10"><label>ci.11.10</label> tataḥ
  priyaṅgvanantāyūthikāpadmātrāyantikālohitikāmbaṣṭhādāḍimatvakśālaparṇīpadmatuṅgakeśaradhātakīvakulaśālmalīśrīveṣṭakamocaraseṣv ariṣṭānayaskṛtīrlehānāsavāṃś ca
  kurvīta;
  śṛṅgāṭakagiloḍyavisamṛṇālakāśakaserukamadhukāmrajambvasanatiniśakakubhakaṭvaṅgarodhrabhallātakapalāśacarmavṛkṣagirikarṇikāśītaśivaniculadāḍimājakarṇaharivṛkṣarājādanagopaghoṇṭāvikaṅgateṣu
  vā; yavānnavikārāṃś ca seveta; yathoktakaṣāyasiddhāṃ yavāgūṃ cāsmai
  prayacchet, kaṣāyāṇi vā pātum || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.11.11"><label>ci.11.11</label>
  mahādhanamahitāhāramauṣadhadveṣiṇamīśvaraṃ vā
  pāṭhābhayācitrakapragāḍhamanalpamākṣikamanyatamamāsavaṃ pāyayet,
  aṅgāaraśūlyopadaṃśaṃ vā mādhvīkamabhīkṣṇaṃ, kṣaudrakapitthamaricānuviddhāni
  cāsmai pānabhojanānyupaharet, uṣṭrāśvatarakharapurīṣacūrṇāni cāsmai
  dadyādaśaneṣu; hiṅgusaindhavayuktair yūṣaiḥ sārṣapaiś ca rāgair bhojayet ;
  aviruddhāni cāsmai pānabhojanānyupaharedrasagandhavanti ca; pravṛddhamehāstu
  vyāyāmaniyuddhakrīḍāgajaturagarathapadāticaryāparikramaṇānyastropāstre<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> vā severan || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.11.12"><label>ci.11.12</label> adhanastvabāndhavo vā
  pādatrāṇātapatravirahito bhaikṣyāśī grāmaikarātravāsī muniriva saṃyatātmā
  yojanaśatamadhikaṃ vā gacchet, mahādhano vā
  śyāmākanīvāravṛttirāmalakakapitthatindukāśmantakaphalāhāro mṛgaiḥ saha
  vaset, tanmūtraśakṛdbhakṣaḥ satatamanuvrajedgāḥ, brahmaṇo vā
  śiloñchavṛttirbhūtvā brahmarathamuddharet, kṛṣet satatamitaraḥ khanedvā
  kūpaṃ, kṛśaṃ tu satataṃ rakṣet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.11.13"><label>ci.11.13</label> bhavati cātra adhano
  vaidyasandeśādevaṃ kurvannatandritaḥ | saṃvatsarādantarādvā pramehāt
  pratimucyate ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne pramehacikitsitaṃ
  nāmaikadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||11 || </p>
 </div>
 <div n="12" type="adhyāya">
  <head>dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.1"><label>ci.12.1</label> athātaḥ pramehapiḍakācikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.2"><label>ci.12.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.3"><label>ci.12.3</label> śarāvikādyā nava piḍakāḥ prāguktāḥ;
  tāḥ prāṇavato 'lpāstvaṅmāṃsaprāptā mṛdvyo 'lparujaḥ kṣiprapākabhedinyaś ca
  sādhyāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.4"><label>ci.12.4</label> tābhir upadrutaṃ pramehiṇam upacaret |
  tatra pūrvarūpeṣv apatarpaṇaṃ vanaspatikaṣāyaṃ bastamūtraṃ copadiśet;
  evamakurvatastasaya madhurāhārasya mūtraṃ svedaḥ śleṣmā ca madhurībhavati
  pramehaś cābhivyakto bhavati, tatrobhayataḥ saṃśodhanamāseveta;
  evamakurvatas tasya doṣāḥ pravṛddhā māṃsaśoṇite pradūṣya śophaṃ
  janayantyupadravān vā kāṃścit, tatroktaḥ pratīkāraḥ sirāmokṣaś ca;
  evamakurvatas tasya śopho vṛddho 'timātraṃ rujo vidāhamāpadyate, tatra
  śastrapraṇidhānamuktaṃ vraṇakriyopasevā ca; evamakurvatas tasya
  pūyo 'bhyantaramavadāryotsaṅgaṃ mahāntamavakāśaṃ kṛtvā pravṛddho
  bhavatyasādhyaḥ; tasmād ādita eva pramehiṇam upakramet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.5"><label>ci.12.5</label>
  bhallātakabilvāmbupippalīmūlodakīryāvarṣābhūpunarnavācitrakaśaṭīsnuhīvaruṇakapuṣkaradantīpathyā
  daśapalonmitā yavakolakulatthāṃś ca prāsthikān saliladroṇe niṣkvāthya
  caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭe 'vatārya
  vacātrivṛtkampillakabhārgīniculaśuṇṭhīgajapippalīviḍaṅgarodhraśirīṣāṇāṃ
  bhāgair ardhapalikair ghṛtaprasthaṃ
  vipācayenmehaśvayathukuṣṭhagulmodarārśaḥplīhavidradhipiḍakānāṃ nāśanaṃ nāmnā
  dhānvantaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.6"><label>ci.12.6</label> durvirecyā hi madhumehino bhavanti
  medo 'bhivyāptaśarīratvāt , tasmāt tīkṣṇameteṣāṃ śodhanaṃ kurvīta |
  piḍakāpīḍitāḥ sopadravāḥ sarva eva pramehā mūtrādimādhurye
  madhugandhasāmānyāt pāribhāṣikīṃ madhumehākhyāṃ labhante || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.7"><label>ci.12.7</label> na caitān kathaṃcidapi svedayet,
  medobahutvād eteṣāṃ viśīryate dehaḥ svedena || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.8"><label>ci.12.8</label> rasāyanīnāṃ ca
  daurbalyānnordhvamuttiṣṭhanti pramehiṇāṃ doṣāḥ, tato madhumehināmadhaḥkāye
  piḍakāḥ prādurbhavanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.9"><label>ci.12.9</label> apakvānāṃ tu piḍakānāṃ śophavat
  pratīkāraḥ, pakvānāṃ vraṇavaditi; tailaṃ tu vraṇaropaṇamevādau kurvīta,
  āragvadhādikaṣāyamutsādanārthe, śālasārādikaṣāyaṃ pariṣecane,
  pippalyādikaṣāyaṃ pānabhojaneṣu,
  pāṭhācitrakaśārṅgeṣṭākṣudrābṛhatīsārivāsomavalkasaptaparṇāragvadhakuṭajamūlacūrṇāni
  madhumithāṇi praśnīyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.10"><label>ci.12.10</label> śālasārādivargakaṣāyaṃ
  caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭamavatārya parisrāvya punarupanīya sādhayet, sidhyati
  cāmalakarodhrapriyaṅgudantīkṛṣṇāyastāmracūrṇānyāvapet, etadanupadagdhaṃ
  lehībhūtamavatāryānuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tato yathāyogam upayuñjīta, eṣa lehaḥ
  sarvamehānāṃ hantā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.11"><label>ci.12.11</label>
  triphalānitrakatrikaṭukaviḍaṅgamustānāṃ nava bhāgāstāvanta eva
  kṛṣṇāyaścūrṇasya, tat sarvamaikadhyaṃ kṛtvā yathāyogaṃ mātrāṃ
  sarpirmadhubhyāṃ saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta, etannavāyasam; etena jāṭharyaṃ na
  bhavati, sanno 'gnirāpyāyate,
  durnāmaśophapāṇḍukuṣṭharogāvipākakāsaśvāsapramehāś ca na bhavanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.12"><label>ci.12.12</label> śālasārādiniryūhe
  caturthāṃśāvaśeṣite | parisrute tataḥ śīte madhu mākṣikamāvapet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.13"><label>ci.12.13</label> phāṇitībhāvamāpannaṃ guḍaṃ
  śodhitam eva ca | ślakṣṇapiṣṭāni cūrṇāni pippalyādigaṇasya ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.14"><label>ci.12.14</label> aikadhyamāvapet kumbhe saṃskṛte
  ghṛtabhāvaite | pippalīcūrṇamadhubhiḥ pralipte 'ntaḥśucau dṛḍhe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.15"><label>ci.12.15</label> ślakṣṇāni tīkṣṇalohasya tatra
  patrāṇi buddhimān | khadirāṅgārataptāni bahuśaḥ sannipātayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.16"><label>ci.12.16</label> supidhānaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā yavapalle
  nidhāpayet | māsāṃstrīṃś caturo vā 'pi yāvadālohasaṃkṣayāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.17"><label>ci.12.17</label> tato jātarasaṃ taṃ tu prātaḥ
  prātar yathābalam | niṣeveta yathāyogamāhāraṃ cāsya kalpayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.18"><label>ci.12.18</label> kārśyakṛdbalināmeṣa sannasyāgneḥ
  prasādhakaḥ | śophanudgulmahṛt kuṣṭhamehapāṇḍvāmayāpahaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.19"><label>ci.12.19</label> plīhodaraharaḥ śīghraṃ
  viṣamajvaranāśanaḥ | abhiṣyandāpaharaṇo lohāriṣṭo mahāguṇaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.12.20"><label>ci.12.20</label> pramehiṇo yadā
  mūtramapicchilamanāvilam | viśadaṃ tiktakaṭukaṃ tadā++ārogyaṃ
  pracakṣate ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne pramehapiḍakācikitsitaṃ
  nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||12 ||</p>
 </div>


 <div n="13" type="adhyāya">
  <head>trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.1"><label>ci.13.1</label> athāto madhumehacikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.2"><label>ci.13.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.3"><label>ci.13.3</label> madhumehitvamāpannaṃ bhiṣagbhiḥ
  parivarjitam | yogenānena matimān pramehiṇamupācaret || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.4"><label>ci.13.4</label> māse śukre śucau caiva śailāḥ
  sūryāṃśutāpitāḥ | jatuprakāśaṃ svarasaṃ śilābhyaḥ prasravanti hi || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.5"><label>ci.13.5</label> śilājatviti vikhyātaṃ
  sarvavyādhivināśanam | trapvādīnāṃ tu lohānāṃ ṣaṇṇāmanyatamānvayam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.6"><label>ci.13.6</label> jñeyaṃ svagandhataś cāpi ṣaḍyoni
  prathitaṃ kṣitau | lohādbhavati tadyasmācchilājatu jatuprabham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.7"><label>ci.13.7</label> tasya lohasya tadvīryaṃ rasaṃ cāpi
  bibharti tat |
  trapusīsāyasādīni pradhānānyuttarottaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.8"><label>ci.13.8</label> yathā tathā prayoge 'pi śreṣṭhe
  śreṣṭhaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ | tat sarvaṃ tiktakaṭukaṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ saram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.9"><label>ci.13.9</label> kaṭupākyuṣṇavīryaṃ ca śoṣaṇaṃ
  chedanaṃ tathā | teṣu yat kṛṣṇamalaghu snigdhaṃ niḥśarkaraṃ ca yat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.10"><label>ci.13.10</label> gomūtragandhi yac cāpi tat
  pradhānaṃ pracakṣate | tadbhāvitaṃ sāragaṇair hṛtadoṣo dinodaye || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.11"><label>ci.13.11</label> pibet sārodakenaiva ślakṣṇapiṣṭaṃ
  yathābalam | jāṅgalena rasenānnaṃ tasmiñjīrṇe tu bhojayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.12"><label>ci.13.12</label> upayujya tulāmevaṃ
  girijādamṛtopamāt | vapurvarṇabalopeto madhumehavivarjitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.13"><label>ci.13.13</label> jīvedvarṣaśataṃ
  pūrṇamajaro 'marasannibhaḥ | śataṃ śataṃ tulāyāṃ tu sahasraṃ daśataulike || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.14"><label>ci.13.14</label> bhallātakavidhānena
  parihāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ | mehaṃ kuṣṭhamapasmāramunmādaṃ ślīpadaṃ garam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.15"><label>ci.13.15</label> śoṣaṃ śophārśasī gulmaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ
  viṣamajvaram | apohatyacirātkālācchilājatu niṣevitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.16"><label>ci.13.16</label> na so 'sti rogo yaṃ cāpi
  nihanyānna śilājatu | śarkarāṃ cirasaṃbhūtāṃ bhinatti ca tathā 'śmarīm || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.17"><label>ci.13.17</label> bhāvanāloḍane cāsya kartavye
  bheṣajair hitaiḥ | evaṃ ca mākṣikaṃ dhātuṃ tāpījamamṛtopamam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.18"><label>ci.13.18</label> madhuraṃ kāñcanābhāsamamlaṃ vā
  rajataprabham | piban hanti jarākuṣṭhamehapāṇḍvāmayakṣayān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.19"><label>ci.13.19</label> tadbhāvitaḥ kapotāṃś ca kulatthāṃś
  ca vivarjayet | pañcakarmaguṇātītaṃ śraddhāvantaṃ jijīviṣum || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.20"><label>ci.13.20</label> yogenānena matimān sādhayed api
  kuṣṭhanam | vṛkṣāstuvarakā ye syuḥ paścimārṇavabhūmiṣu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.21"><label>ci.13.21</label>
  vīcītaraṅgavikṣepamārutoddhūtapallavāḥ | teṣāṃ phalāni gṛhṇīyāt
  supakvānyambudāgame || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.22"><label>ci.13.22</label>
  majjāṃ tebhyo 'pi saṃhṛtya
  śoṣayitvā vicūrṇya ca | tilavat pīḍayed droṇyāṃ srāvayed vā kusumbhavat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.23"><label>ci.13.23</label> tattailaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ
  pacedātoyasaṃkṣayāt | avatārya karīṣe ca pakṣamātraṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.24"><label>ci.13.24</label> snigdhaḥ svinno hṛtamalaḥ
  pakṣādūrdhvaṃ prayatnavān | caturthabhaktāntaritaḥ śuklādau divase śubhe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.25"><label>ci.13.25</label> mantrapūtasya tailasya
  pibenmātrāṃ yathābalam | tatra mantraṃ pravakṣyāmi yenedam abhimantryate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.26"><label>ci.13.26</label> majjasāra mahāvīrya sarvān dhātūn
  viśodhaya | śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇistvāmājñāpayate 'cyutaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.27"><label>ci.13.27</label> tenāsyor dhvamadhaś cāpi doṣā
  yāntyasakṛttataḥ | asnehalavaṇāṃ sāyaṃ yavāgūṃ śītalāṃ pibet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.28"><label>ci.13.28</label> pañcāhaṃ prapibettailamanena
  vidhinā naraḥ | pakṣaṃ pariharec cāpi mudgayūṣaudanāśanaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.29"><label>ci.13.29</label> pañcabhir divasair evaṃ
  sarvakuṣṭhair vimucyate | tad eva khadirakvāthe triguṇe sādhu sādhitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.30"><label>ci.13.30</label> nihitaṃ pūrvavat <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>pakṣāt pibenmāsamatandritaḥ |
  tenābhyaktaśarīraś ca kurvītāhāramīritam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.31"><label>ci.13.31</label> bhinnasvaraṃ raktanetraṃ viśīrṇaṃ
  kṛmibhakṣitam | anenāśu prayogeṇa sādhayet kuṣṭhinaṃ naram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.32"><label>ci.13.32</label> sarpirmadhuyutaṃ pītaṃ tadeva
  khadirāmbunā | pakṣimāṃsarasāhāraṃ karoti dviśatāyuṣam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.33"><label>ci.13.33</label> tad eva nasye
  pañcāśaddivasānupayojitam | vapuṣmantaṃ śrutidharaṃ karoti triśatāyuṣam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.34"><label>ci.13.34</label> śodhayanti naraṃ pītā
  majjānastasya mātrayā | mahāvīryastuvarakaḥ kuṣṭhamehāpahaḥ paraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.13.35"><label>ci.13.35</label> sāntardhūmastasya majjā tu
  dagdhaḥ kṣiptastaile saindhavaṃ cāñjanaṃ ca | paillyaṃ
  hanyādarmanaktāndhyakācān nīlīrogaṃ taimiraṃ cāñjanena ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne madhumehacikitsitaṃ nāma
  trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||13 ||</p>
 </div>
 <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
  <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.1"><label>ci.14.1</label> athāta udarāṇāṃ cikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.2"><label>ci.14.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.3"><label>ci.14.3</label> aṣṭāvudarāṇi pūrvamuddiṣṭāni |
  teṣv asādhyaṃ baddhagudaṃ parisrāvi ca; avaśiṣṭāni kṛcchrasādhyāni;
  sarvāṇyeva pratyākhyāyopakrameta | teṣv ādyaś caturvargo bheṣajasādhyaḥ,
  uttaraḥ śastrasādhyaḥ, kālaprakarṣāt sarvāṇyeva śastrasādhyāni
  varjayitavyāni vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.4"><label>ci.14.4</label> udarī tu
  gurvabhiṣyandirūkṣavidāhisnigdhapiśitapariṣekāvagāhān pariharet;
  śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmanīvārān nityamaśnīyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.5"><label>ci.14.5</label> tatra vātodariṇaṃ
  vidārigandhādisiddhena sarpiṣā snehayitvā, tilvakavipakvenānulomya,
  citrāphalatailapragāḍhena vidārigandādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayecca,
  sālvaṇena copanāhayed udaraṃ, bhojayeccainaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena kṣīreṇa
  jāṅgalarasena ca, svedayeccābhīkṣṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.6"><label>ci.14.6</label> pittodariṇaṃ tu
  madhuragaṇavipakvena sarpiṣā snehayitvā,
  śyāmātriphalātrivṛdvipakvenānulomya, śarkarāmadhughṛtapragāḍhena
  nyagrodhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayecca, pāyasenopanāhayed udaraṃ,
  bhojayeccainaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena payasā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.7"><label>ci.14.7</label> śleṣmodariṇaṃ tu
  pippalyādikaṣāyasiddhena sarpiṣopasnehya, snuhīkṣīravipakvenānulomya,
  trikaṭukamūtrakṣāratailapragāḍhena muṣkakādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayecca,
  śaṇātasīdhātakīkiṇvasarṣapamūlakabījakalkaiścopanāhayed udaraṃ,
  bhojayeccainaṃ trikaṭukapragāḍhena kulatthayūṣeṇa pāyasena vā,
  svedayeccābhīkṣṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.8"><label>ci.14.8</label> dūṣyodariṇaṃ tu pratyākhyāya
  saptalāśaṅkhinīsvarasasiddhena sarpiṣā viracayen māsam ardhamāsaṃ vā,
  mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasurāgomūtrasiddhena vā; śuddhakoṣṭhaṃ tu
  madyenāśvamārakaguñjākākādanīmūlakalkaṃ pāyayet; ikṣukāṇḍāni vā kṛṣṇasarpeṇa
  daṃśayitvā bhakṣayed vallīphalāni vā, mūlajaṃ kandajaṃ vā viṣamā sevayet,
  tenāgado bhavaty anyaṃ vā bhāvam āpadyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.9"><label>ci.14.9</label> bhavati cātra kupitānilamūlatvāt 
  saṃcitatvān malasya ca |
  sarvodareṣu śaṃsanti bahuśas tv anulomanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.10"><label>ci.14.10</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ sāmānyayogān
  vakṣyāmaḥ | tadyathā eraṇḍatailam aharahar māsaṃ dvau vā kevalaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ
  kṣīrayuktaṃ vā sevetodakavarjī, māhiṣaṃ vā mūtraṃ kṣīreṇa nirāhāraḥ
  saptarātram, uṣṭrīkṣīrāhāro vā 'nnavārivarjī pakṣaṃ, pippalīṃ vā māsaṃ
  pūrvoktena vidhānenāseveta, saindhavājamodāyuktaṃ vā nikumbhatailam,
  ārdraśṛṅgaverarasapātraśatasiddhaṃ vā vātaśūle 'vacāryaṃ,
  śṛṅgaverarasavipakvaṃ kṣīramāseveta, cavyaśṛṅgaverakalkaṃ vā payasā
  saraladevadārucitrakam eva vā, muraṅgīśālaparṇīśyāmāpunarnavākalkaṃ vā,
  jyotiṣkaphalatailaṃ vā kṣīreṇa svarjikāhiṅgumiśraṃ pibet, <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>guḍadvitīyāṃ vā harītakīṃ
  bhakṣayet, srutīkṣīrabhāvitānāṃ vā pippalīnāṃ sahasraṃ kālena,
  pathyākṛṣṇācūrṇaṃ vā snuhīkṣīrabhāvitamutkārikāṃ pakvāṃ dāpayet;
  harītakīcūrṇaṃ prasthamāḍhake ghṛtasyāvāpyāṅgāreṣv abhivilāpya
  khajenābhimathyānuguptaṃ kṛtvā 'rdhamāsaṃ yavapalle vāsayet, tataścoddhṛtya
  parisrāvya harītakīkvāthāmladadhīnyāvāpya vipacet, tadyathāyogaṃ
  māsamardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet; gavye payasi mahāvṛkṣakṣīramāvāpya vipacet,
  vipakvaṃ cāvatārya śītībhūtaṃ manthānenābhimathya navanītamādāya bhūyo
  mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇaiva vipacet, tadyathāyogaṃ māsaṃ māsārdhaṃ vā pāyayet;
  cavyacitrakadantyativiṣākuṣṭhasārivātriphalājamodaharidrāśaṅkhinītrivṛttrikaṭukānāmardhakārṣikā
  bhāgā, rājavṛkṣaphalamajjñāmaṣṭau karṣāḥ, mahāvṛkṣakṣīrapaledve, gavāṃ
  kṣīramūtrayor aṣṭāvaṣṭau palāni, etat sarvaṃ ghṛtaprasthe samāvāpya vipacet,
  tadyathāyogaṃ māsamardhamāsṃ vā pāyayet; etāni tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni
  sarpīṣyudaragulmavidradhyaṣṭhīlānāhakuṣṭhonmādāpasmāreṣūpayojyāni
  virecanārthaṃ; mūtrāsavāriṣṭasurāś cābhīkṣṇaṃ mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasaṃbhṛtāḥ seveta;
  virecanadravyakaṣāyaṃ vā śṛṅgaveradevadārupragāḍham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.11"><label>ci.14.11</label>
  vamanavirecanaśirovirecanadravyāṇāṃ pālikābhāgāḥ
  pippalyādivacādiharidrādiparipaṭhitānāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ ślakṣṇapiṣṭānāṃ
  yathoktānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tat sarvaṃ mūtragaṇe prakṣipya
  mahāvṛkṣakṣīraprasthaṃ ca mṛdvagninā 'vaghaṭṭayan vipacedapradagdhakalkaṃ,
  tatsādhusiddhamavatārya śītībhūtamakṣamātrā guṭikā vartayet, tāsāmekāṃ dve
  tisro vā guṭikā balāpekṣayā māsāṃstrīṃś caturo vā seveta, eṣā++<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>ānāhavartikriyā viśeṣeṇa
  mahāvyādhiṣūpayujyate (viśeṣeṇa) koṣṭhajāṃś ca kṛmīnapahanti
  kāsaśvāsakṛmikuṣṭhapratiśyāyārocakāvipākodāvartāṃś ca nāśayati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.12"><label>ci.14.12</label>
  madanaphalamajjakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārgavatrivṛttrikaṭukasarṣapalavaṇāni
  mahāvṛkṣakṣīramūtrayor anyatareṇa piṣṭvā 'ṅguṣṭhamātrāṃ vartiṃ kṛtvodariṇa
  ānāhe tailalavaṇābhyaktagudasyaikāṃ dve tisro vā pāyau nidadhyāt,
  eṣā++ānāhavartikriyā vātamūtrapurīṣodāvartādhmānānāheṣu vidheyā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.13"><label>ci.14.13</label> plīhodariṇaḥ snigdhasvinnasya
  dadhnā bhuktavato vāmabāhau kūrparābhyantarataḥ sirāṃ vidhyet, vimardayecca
  pāṇinā plīhānaṃ rudhirasyandanārthaṃ; tataḥ saṃśuddhadehaṃ
  samudraśuktikākṣāraṃ payasā pāyayeta, hiṅgusauvarcike vā kṣīreṇa, srutena
  palāśakṣāreṇa vā yavakṣāraṃ, kiṃśukakṣārodakena vā bahuśaḥ srutena
  yavakṣāraṃ, pārijātakekṣurakāpāmārgakṣāraṃ vā, tailasṃsṛṣṭaṃ
  śobhāñjanakayūṣaṃ pippalīsaindhavacitrakayuktaṃ, pūtikarañjakṣāraṃ
  vā 'mlasrutaṃ viḍlavaṇapippalīprāgāḍham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.14"><label>ci.14.14</label>
  pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakaśṛṅgaverayavakṣārasaindhavānāṃ pālikā bhāgāḥ,
  ghṛtaprasthaṃ tattulyaṃ ca kṣīraṃ tadaikadhyaṃ vipācayet , etat ṣaṭpalakaṃ
  nāma sarpiḥ
  plīhāgnisaṅgagulmodarodāvartaśvayathupāṇḍurogakāsaśvāsapratiśyāyor dhvavātaviṣamajvarānapahanti |
  mandāgnirvā hiṅgvādikaṃ cūrṇam upayuñjīta || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.15"><label>ci.14.15</label> yakṛddālye 'pyeṣa eva
  kriyāvibhāgaḥ | viśeṣatas tu dakṣiṇabāhau sirāvyadhaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.16"><label>ci.14.16</label> maṇibandhaṃ sakṛnnāmya
  vāmāṅguṣṭhasamīritām | dahet sirāṃ śareṇāśu plīhno vaidyaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.17"><label>ci.14.17</label> baddhagude parisrāviṇi ca
  snigdhasvinnasyābhyaktasyādho nābhervāmataś caturaṅgulamapahāya romarājyā
  udaraṃ pāṭayitvā caturaṅgulapramāṇamantrāṇi niṣkṛṣya nirīkṣya
  baddhagudasyāntrapratirodhakaramaśmānaṃ bālaṃ vā 'pohya malajātaṃ vā tato
  madhusarpirbhyām abhyajyāntrāṇi yathāsthānaṃ sthāpayitvā <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>bāhyaṃ vraṇamudarasya sīvyet |
  parisrāviṇyapyevam eva śalyamuddhṛtyāntrasrāvān saṃśodhya<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>, tacchidramāntraṃ samādhāya
  kālapipīlikābhir daṃśayet, daṣṭe ca tāsāṃ kāyānapaharenna śirāṃsi, tataḥ
  pūrvavat sīvyet, saṃdhānaṃ ca yathoktaṃ kārayet, yaṣṭīmadhukamiśrayā ca
  kṛṣṇamṛdā 'valipya bandhenopacaret, tato nivātamāgāraṃ
  praveśyācārikam upadiśet, vāsayeccainaṃ tailadroṇyāṃ sarpirdroṇyāṃ vā
  payovṛttim iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.18"><label>ci.14.18</label>
  dakodariṇastu
  vātaharatailābhyaktasyoṣṇodakasvinnasya sthitasyāptaiḥ suparigṛhītasyākakṣāt
  pariveṣṭitasyādhonābhervāmataś caturaṅgulamapahāya romarājyā
  vrīhimukhenāṅguṣṭhodarapramāṇamavagāḍhaṃ vidhyet, tatra
  trapvādīnāmanyatamasya nāḍīṃ dvidvārāṃ pakṣanāḍīṃ vā saṃyojya
  doṣodakamavasiñcet, toto nāḍīmapahṛtya tailalavaṇenābhyajya vraṇaṃ
  bandhenopacaret, na caikasminn eva divase sarvaṃ doṣodakamapaharet, sahasā
  hy apahṛte tṛṣṇājvarāṅgamardātīsāraśvāsakāsapādadāhā utpadyerannāpūryate vā
  bhṛśataramudaramasañjātaprāṇasya,
  tasmāt tṛtīyacaturthapañcamaṣaṣṭhāṣṭamadaśamadvādaśaṣoḍaśarātrāṇāmanyatamamantarīkṛtya
  doṣodakamalpālpamavasiñcet; niḥsṛte ca doṣe
  gāḍhataramāvikakauśeyacarmaṇāmanyatamena pariveṣṭayed udaraṃ, tathā
  nādhmāpayati vāyuḥ; ṣaṇmāsāṃś ca payasā bhojayejjāṅgalarasena vā,
  tatastrīnmāsānardhodakena payasā phalāmlena jāṅgalarasena vā, avaśiṣṭaṃ
  māsatrayamannaṃ laghu hitaṃ vā seveta, evaṃ saṃvatsareṇāgado bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.14.19"><label>ci.14.19</label> bhavati cātra āsthāpane caiva
  virecane ca pāne tathā++āhāravidhikriyāsu | sarvodaribhyaḥ kuśalaiḥ prayojyaṃ
  kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ jāṅgalajo raso vā ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne udaracikitsitaṃ nāma
  caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||14 ||</p>
 </div>
 <div n="15" type="adhyāya">
  <head>pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.1"><label>ci.15.1</label> athāto mūḍhagarbhacikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.2"><label>ci.15.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.3"><label>ci.15.3</label> nāto 'nyat kaṣṭatamamasti yathā
  mūḍhagarbhaśalyoddharaṇam; atra hi yoniyakṛtplīhāntravivaragarbhāśayānāṃ
  madhye karma kartavyaṃ sparśena,
  utkarṣaṇāpakarṣaṇasthānāpavartanotkartanabhedanacchedanapīḍanarjūkaraṇadāraṇāni
  caikahastena garbhaṃ garbhiṇīṃ cāhiṃsatā, tasmād adhipatimāpṛcchya paraṃ ca
  yatnamāsthāyopakrameta || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.4"><label>ci.15.4</label> tatra samāsenāṣṭavidhā
  mūḍhagarbhagatiruddiṣṭā; svabhāvagatā api trayaḥ saṅgā bhavanti śiraso
  vaiguṇyādaṃsayor jaghanasya vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.5"><label>ci.15.5</label> jīvati tu garbhe
  sūtikāgarbhanirharaṇe prayateta | nirhartumaśakye cyāvanān mantrānupaśṛṇuyāt;
  tān vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.6"><label>ci.15.6</label> ihāmṛtaṃ ca somaś ca citrabhānuś ca
  bhāmini | uccaiḥśravāś ca turago mandire nivasantu te || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.7"><label>ci.15.7</label> idamamṛtamapāṃ samuddhṛtaṃ vai tava
  laghu garbhamimaṃ pramuñcatu stri | tadanalapavanārkavāsavāste saha
  lavaṇāmbudharair diśantu śāntim || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.8"><label>ci.15.8</label> muktāḥ paśorvipāśāś ca muktāḥ
  sūryeṇa raśmayaḥ | muktaḥ sarvabhayād garbha ehyehi viramāvitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.9"><label>ci.15.9</label> auṣadhāni ca vidadhyādyathoktāni |
  mṛte cottānāyā ābhugnasakthyā vastrādhārakonnamitakaṭhyā <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker"
  >*</ref>dhanvananagavṛttikāśālmalīmṛtsnaghṛtābhyāṃ mrakṣayitvā hastaṃ yonau
  praveśya garbham upaharet | tatra sakthibhyām āgatamanulomamevāñchet,
  ekasakthnā pratipannasyetarasakthi prasāryāpaharet, sphigdeśenāgatasya
  sphigdeśaṃ prapīḍyor dhvamutkṣipya sakthinī prasāryāpaharet, tiryagāgatasya
  parighasyeva tiraścīnasya paś cād ardhamūrdhvamutkṣipya pūrvārdhamapatyapathaṃ
  pratyārjavamānīyāpaharet, pārśvāpavṛttaśirasamaṃsaṃ prapīḍyor dhvamutkṣipya
  śiro 'patyapathamānīyāpaharet, bāhudvayapratipannasyor dhvamutpīḍyāṃsau
  śiro 'nulomamānīyāpaharet, dvāvantyāvasādhyau mūḍhagarbhau, evamaśakye
  śastramavacārayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.10"><label>ci.15.10</label> sacetanaṃ ca śastreṇa na
  kathañcana dārayet | dāryamāṇo hi jananīmātmānaṃ caiva ghātayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.11"><label>ci.15.11</label> aviṣahye vikāre tu śreyo
  garbhasya pātanam | na garbhiṇyā viparyāsastasmāt prāptaṃ na hāpayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.12"><label>ci.15.12</label> tataḥ striyamāśvāsya
  maṇḍalāgreṇāṅgulīśastreṇa vā śiro vidārya, śiraḥkapālānyāhṛtya, śaṅkunā
  gṛhītvorasi kakṣāyāṃ vā 'paharet; abhinnaśirasamakṣikūṭe gaṇḍe vā,
  aṃsasaṃsaktasyāṃsadeśe bāhū chittvā, dṛtimivātataṃ vātapūrṇodaraṃ vā vidārya
  nirasyāntrāṇi śithilībhūtamāharet, jaghanasaktasya vā jaghanakapālānīti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.13"><label>ci.15.13</label> kiṃbahunā yadyadaṅgaṃ hi
  garbhasya tasya sajjati tadbhiṣak | samyagvinirharecchittvā rakṣennārīṃ ca
  yatnataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.14"><label>ci.15.14</label> garbhasya gatayaścitrā
  jāyante 'nilakopataḥ | tatrānalpamatirvaidyo varteta vidhipūrvakam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.15"><label>ci.15.15</label> nopekṣeta mṛtaṃ garbhaṃ
  muhūrtam api paṇḍitaḥ | sa hyāśu jananīṃ hanti nirucchvāsaṃ paśuṃ yathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.16"><label>ci.15.16</label> maṇḍalāgreṇa kartavyaṃ
  chedyamantarvijānatā | vṛddhipatraṃ hi tīkṣṇāgraṃ nārīṃ hiṃsyāt kadācana || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.17"><label>ci.15.17</label> athāpatantīmaparāṃ pātayet
  pūrvavadbhiṣak | hastenāpaharedvā 'pi pārśvabhyāṃ paripīḍya vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.18"><label>ci.15.18</label> dhunuyāc ca muhurnārīṃ
  pīḍayed vā 'ṃsapiṇḍikām |
  tailāktayonerevaṃ tāṃ pātayenmatimān bhiṣak || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.19"><label>ci.15.19</label> evaṃ nirhṛtaśalyāṃ tu
  siñceduṣṇena vāriṇā | tato 'bhyaktaśarīrāyā yonau snehaṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.20"><label>ci.15.20</label> evaṃ mṛdvī bhaved yonistacchūlaṃ
  copaśāmyati | kṛṣṇātanmūlaśuṇṭhyelāhiṅgubhārgīḥ sadīpyakāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.21"><label>ci.15.21</label> vacāmativiṣāṃ rāsnāṃ cavyaṃ
  saṃcūrṇya pāyayet | snehena doṣasyandārthaṃ vedanopaśamāya ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.22"><label>ci.15.22</label> kvāthaṃ caiṣāṃ tathā kalkaṃ
  cūrṇaṃ vā snehavarjitam | śākatvagghiṅgvativiṣāpāṭhākaṭukarohiṇīḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.23"><label>ci.15.23</label> tathā tejovatīṃ cāpi pāyayet
  pūrvavadbhiṣak | trirātraṃ pañcasaptāhaṃ tataḥ snehaṃ punaḥ pibet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.24"><label>ci.15.24</label> pāyayet āsavaṃ naktam ariṣṭaṃ vā
  susaṃskṛtam | śirīṣakakubhābhyāṃ ca toyam ācamane hitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.25"><label>ci.15.25</label> upadravāś ca ye 'nye syustān
  yathāsvamupācaret | sarvataḥ pariśuddhā ca snigdhapathyālpabhojanā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.26"><label>ci.15.26</label> svedābhyaṅgaparā nityaṃ bhavet
  krodhavivarjitā | payo vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ daśāhaṃ bhojane hitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.27"><label>ci.15.27</label> rasaṃ daśāhaṃ śeṣe tu
  yathāyogamupācaret | vyupadravāṃ viśuddhāṃ ca jñātvā ca varavarṇinīm || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.28"><label>ci.15.28</label> ūrdhvaṃ caturbhyo māsebhyo
  visṛjet parihārataḥ | yonisantarpaṇe 'bhyaṅge pāne bastiṣu bhojane || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.29"><label>ci.15.29</label> balātailamidaṃ cāsyai
  dadyādanilavāraṇam | balāmūlakaṣāyasya daśamūlīśṛtasya ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.30"><label>ci.15.30</label> yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvāthasya
  payasas tathā | aṣṭāvaṣṭau śubhā bhāgāstailādekastadekataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.31"><label>ci.15.31</label> pacedāvāpya madhuraṃ gaṇaṃ
  saindhavasaṃyutam | tathā 'guruṃ sarjarasaṃ saralaṃ devadāru ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.32"><label>ci.15.32</label> mañjiṣṭhāṃ candanaṃ kuṣṭhamelāṃ
  kālānusārivām | māṃsīṃ śaileyakaṃ patraṃ tagaraṃ sārivāṃ vacām || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.33"><label>ci.15.33</label> śatāvarīmaśvagandhāṃ śatapuṣpāṃ
  punarnavām | tat sādhusiddhaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mṛnmaye 'pi vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.34"><label>ci.15.34</label> prakṣipya kalaśe samyak
  svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet | balātailamidaṃ khyātaṃ sarvavātavikāranut || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.35"><label>ci.15.35</label> yathābalamato mātrāṃ sūtikāyai
  pradāpayet | yā ca garbhārthinī nārī kṣīṇaśukraś ca yaḥ pumān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.36"><label>ci.15.36</label> vātakṣīṇe marmahate
  mathite 'bhihate tathā | bhagne śramābhipanne ca sarvathaivopayujyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.37"><label>ci.15.37</label> etadākṣepakādīn vai
  vātavyādhīnapohati | hikkāṃ kāsamadhīmanthaṃ gulmaṃ śvāsaṃ ca dustaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.38"><label>ci.15.38</label>
  ṣaṇmāsānupayujyaitadantravṛddhimapohati | pratyagradhātuḥ puruṣo bhavecca
  sthirayauvanaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.39"><label>ci.15.39</label> rājñāmetaddhi kartavyaṃ
  rājamātrāś ca ye narāḥ | sukhinaḥ sukumārāś ca dhaninaś cāpi ye narāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.15.40"><label>ci.15.40</label> balākaṣāyapītebhyastilebhyo
  vā 'pyanekaśaḥ | tailamutpādya  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.8"><label>ci.16.8</label> pañcamūlakaṣāyeṇa prakṣālya
  lavaṇottaraiḥ | tailair bhadrādimadhukasaṃyuktaiḥ pratipūrayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.9"><label>ci.16.9</label> vair ecanikayuktena traivṛtena
  viśodhya ca | pṛthakparṇyādisiddhena traivṛtena ca ropayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.10"><label>ci.16.10</label> paittikaṃ śarkarālājāmadhukaiḥ
  sārivāyutaiḥ | pradihyāt kṣīrapiṣṭair vā payasyośīracandanaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.11"><label>ci.16.11</label> pākyaiḥ śītakaṣāyair vā
  kṣīrair ikṣurasais tathā | jīvanīyaghṛtair vā 'pi secayeccharkarāyutaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.12"><label>ci.16.12</label> trivṛddharītakīnāṃ ca cūrṇaṃ
  lihyānmadhudravam | jalaukobhir hareccāsṛk pakvaṃ cāpaṭhya buddhimān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.13"><label>ci.16.13</label> kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyeṇa
  prakṣālyaudakajena vā | tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukaiḥ sakṣaudraiḥ sarpiṣā yutaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.14"><label>ci.16.14</label> upadihya pratanunā vāsasā
  veṣṭayed vraṇam | prapauṇḍarīkamañjiṣṭhāmadhukośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.15"><label>ci.16.15</label> saharidraiḥ kṛtaṃ sarpiḥ sakṣīraṃ
  vraṇaropaṇam | kṣīraśuklāpṛthakparṇīsamaṅgārodhracandanaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.16"><label>ci.16.16</label> nyagrodhādipravāleṣu teṣāṃ
  tvakṣvathavā kṛtam | naktamālasya patrāṇi taruṇāni phalāni ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.17"><label>ci.16.17</label> sumanāyāś ca patrāṇi
  paṭolāriṣṭayos tathā | dve haridre madhūcchiṣṭaṃ madhukaṃ tiktarohiṇī || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.18"><label>ci.16.18</label> priyaṅguḥ kuśamūlaṃ ca niculasya
  tvageva ca | mañjiṣṭhācandanośīramutpalaṃ sārive trivṛt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.19"><label>ci.16.19</label> eteṣāṃ
  kārṣikair bhāgair ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet | duṣṭavraṇapraśamanaṃ
  nāḍīvraṇaviśodhanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.20"><label>ci.16.20</label> sadyaśchinnavraṇānāṃ ca
  karañjādyamidaṃ śubham | duṣṭavraṇāś ca ye kecidye cotsṛṣṭakriyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.21"><label>ci.16.21</label> nāḍyo gambhīrikā yāś ca
  sadyaścchinnāstathaiva ca | agnikṣārakṛtāś caiva ye vraṇā dāruṇā api || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.22"><label>ci.16.22</label> karañjādyena haviṣā <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>praśāmyanti na saṃśayaḥ |
  iṣṭakāsikatāloṣṭagośakṛttuṣapāṃśubhiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.23"><label>ci.16.23</label> mūtrair uṣṇaiś ca satataṃ
  svedayecchlaṣmavidradhim | kaṣāyapānair vamanairālepair upanāhanaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.24"><label>ci.16.24</label> hareddoṣānabhīkṣṇaṃ
  cāpyalābvā 'sṛk tathaiva ca | āragvadhakaṣāyeṇa pakvaṃ cāpāṭhya dhāvayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.25"><label>ci.16.25</label>
  haridrātrivṛtāśaktutilair madhusamāyutaiḥ | pūrayitvā vraṇaṃ samyagbadhnīyāt
  kīrtitaṃ yathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.26"><label>ci.16.26</label> tataḥ
  kulatthikādantītrivṛcchyāmārkatilvakaiḥ | kuryāt tailaṃ sagomūtraṃ hitaṃ tatra
  sasaindhavam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.27"><label>ci.16.27</label> pittavidradhivat sarvāḥ kriyā
  niravaśeṣataḥ | vidradhyoḥ kuśalaḥ kuryād raktāgantunimittayoḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.28"><label>ci.16.28</label>
  varuṇādigaṇakvāthamapakve 'bhyantarotthite | ūṣakādipratīvāpaṃ pibet
  sukhakaraṃ naraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.29"><label>ci.16.29</label> anayor vargayoḥ siddhaṃ
  sarpirvair ecanena ca | acirādvidradhiṃ hanti prātaḥ prātar niṣevitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.30"><label>ci.16.30</label> ebhir eva gaṇaiś cāpi saṃsiddhaṃ
  snehasaṃyutam | kāryamāsthāpanaṃ kṣipraṃ tathaivāpyanuvāsanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.31"><label>ci.16.31</label> pānālepanabhojyeṣu
  madhuśigrudrumo 'pi vā | dattāvāpo yathādoṣamapakvaṃ hanti vidradhim || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.32"><label>ci.16.32</label> toyadhānyāmlamūtrais tu peyo vā 'pi
  surādibhiḥ | yathādoṣagaṇakvāthaiḥ pibedvā 'pi śilājatu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.33"><label>ci.16.33</label> pradhānaṃ guggulaṃ cāpi śuṇṭhīṃ
  ca suradāru ca | snehopanāhau kuryāc ca sadā cāpyanulomanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.34"><label>ci.16.34</label> yathoddiṣṭāṃ sirāṃ vidhyet
  kaphaje vidradhau bhiṣak | raktapittānilottheṣu kecidbāhau vadanti tu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.35"><label>ci.16.35</label> pakvaṃ vā bahirunnaddhaṃ bhittvā
  vraṇavadācaret | sruteṣūrdhvamadho vā 'pi mair eyāmlasurāsavaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.36"><label>ci.16.36</label> peyo varuṇakādistu
  madhuśigrudrumo 'pi vā | śigrumūlajale siddhaṃ sasiddhārthakam odanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.37"><label>ci.16.37</label> yavakolakulatthānāṃ
  yūṣair bhuñjīta mānavaḥ | prātaḥ prātaś ca seveta mātrayā tailvakaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.38"><label>ci.16.38</label> trivṛtādigaṇakvāthasiddhaṃ
  vā 'pyupaśāntaye | nopagacchedyathāpākaṃ prayateta tathā bhiṣak || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.39"><label>ci.16.39</label> paryāgate vidradhau tu
  siddhirnaikāntikī smṛtā | pratyākhyāya tu kurvīta majjajāte tu vidradhau || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.40"><label>ci.16.40</label> snehasvedopapannānāṃ kuryād 
  raktāvasecana | vidradhyuktāṃ kriyāṃ kuryāt pakve vā 'sthi tu bhedayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.41"><label>ci.16.41</label> niḥśalyamatha vijñāya kartavyaṃ
  vraṇaśodhanam | dhāvettiktakaṣāyeṇa tiktaṃ sarpis tathā hitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.42"><label>ci.16.42</label> yadi majjaparisrāvo na nivarteta
  dehinaḥ | kuryāt saṃśodhanīyāni kaṣāyādīni buddhimān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.16.43"><label>ci.16.43</label> priyaṅgudhātakīrodhrakaṭphalaṃ
  tinisaindhavam | etais tailaṃ vipaktavyaṃ vidradhivraṇaropaṇam ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne vidradhicikitsitaṃ nāma
  ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||16 ||</p>
 </div>
 <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
  <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.1"><label>ci.17.1</label> athāto
  visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.2"><label>ci.17.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.3"><label>ci.17.3</label> sādhyā visarpāstraya ādito ye na
  sannipātakṣatajau hi sādhyau | sādhyeṣu tatpathyagaṇair vidadhyād ghṛtāni
  sekāṃś ca tathopadehān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.4"><label>ci.17.4</label>
  mustāśatāhvāsuradārukuṣṭhavārāhikustumburukṛṣṇagandhāḥ | vātātmako coṣṇagaṇāḥ
  prayojyāḥ sekeṣu lepeṣu tathā sadantīn
  surāṣṭrajāsaindhavasaṃprayuktān | prakṣālane cāpi
  karañjanimbajātyakṣapīlusvarasāḥ prayojyāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.25"><label>ci.17.25</label> suvarcikāsaindhavacitrakeṣu
  nikumbhatālītalarūpikāsu | phaleṣv apāmārgabhaveṣu caiva kuryāt samūtreṣu
  hitāya tailam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.26"><label>ci.17.26</label> nāḍīṃ tu śalyaprabhavāṃ vidārya
  nirhṛtya śalyaṃ praviśodhya mārgam | saṃśodhayet
  kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhais tilais tato ropaṇamāśu kuryāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.27"><label>ci.17.27</label>
  kumbhīkakharjūrakapitthabilvavanaspatīnāṃ ca śalāṭuvargaiḥ | kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ
  vipacet tu tailamāvāpya mustāsaralāpriyaṅgūḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.28"><label>ci.17.28</label> sugandhikāmocarasāhipuṣoaṃ
  rodhraṃ vidadhyādapi dhātakīṃ ca | etena śalyaprabhavā tu nāḍī rohedvraṇo vā
  sukhabhāśu caiva || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.29"><label>ci.17.29</label> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ nāḍī
  marmāśritā ca yā | kṣārasūtreṇa tāṃ cchindyānna tu śastreṇa buddhimān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.30"><label>ci.17.30</label> eṣaṇyā gatimanviṣya
  ārasūtrānusāriṇīm | sūcīṃ nidadhyād gatyante tahonnamyāśu nirharet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.31"><label>ci.17.31</label> sūtrasyāntaṃ samānīya gāḍhaṃ
  bandhaṃ samācaret | tataḥ kṣārabalaṃ vīkṣya sūtramanyat praveśayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.32"><label>ci.17.32</label> kṣārāktaṃ matimān vaidyo yāvanna
  chidyate gatiḥ |
  bhagandare 'pyeṣa vidhiḥ kāryo vaidyena jānatā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.33"><label>ci.17.33</label> sūcībhir yavavaktrābhir ācitān vā
  samantataḥ | mūle sūtreṇa badhnīyācchinne copavaredvraṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.34"><label>ci.17.34</label> yā dvivraṇīye 'bhihitāstu
  vartyastāḥ sarvanāḍīṣu bhiṣagvidadhyāt | ghoṇṭāphalatvaglavaṇāni
  lākṣāpūgīphalaṃ cālavaṇaṃ ca patram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.35"><label>ci.17.35</label> sruhyarkadugdhena tu kalka eṣa
  vartīkṛto hantyacireṇa nāḍīḥ | bibhītakāmrāsthivaṭapravālā
  hareṇukāśaṅkhinibījamasyaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.36"><label>ci.17.36</label> vārāhikandaś ca tathā pradeyo
  nāḍīṣu tailena ca miśrayitvā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.37"><label>ci.17.37</label> dhattūrajaṃ madanakodravajaṃ ca
  bījaṃ kośātakī śukanasā mṛgabhojinī ca | aṅkoṭabījakusumaṃ gatiṣu prayojyaṃ
  lākṣodakāhṛtamalāsu vikṛtya
  cūrṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.38"><label>ci.17.38</label> tathā ca gomāṃsamasīṃ hitāya
  koṣṭhāśritasyādarato diśanti | varīkṛtaṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktaṃ nāḍīghnamuktaṃ
  lavaṇottamaṃ vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.39"><label>ci.17.39</label> duṣṭavraṇe yadvihitaṃ ca tailaṃ
  tat sarvanāḍīṣu bhiṣagvidadhyāt | cūrṇīkṛtair atha vimiśritamebhir eva tailaṃ
  prayuktamacireṇa gatiṃ nihanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.40"><label>ci.17.40</label> eṣveva mūtrasahiteṣu vidhāya
  tailaṃ tat sādhitaṃ gatimapohati saptarātrāt | piṇḍītakasya tu
  varāhavibhāvitasya mūleṣu kandaśakaleṣu ca sauvaheṣu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.41"><label>ci.17.41</label> tailaṃ kṛtaṃ gatimapohati
  śīghrametat kandeṣu cāmaravarāyudhasāhvayeṣu |
  bhallātakārkamaricair lavaṇottamena siddhaṃ viḍaṅgarajanīdvayacitrakaiś ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.42"><label>ci.17.42</label> syan mārkavasya ca rasena nihanti
  tailaṃ nāḍīṃ kaphānilakṛtāmapacīṃ vraṇāṃś ca | stanye gate vikṛtimāśu bhiṣak
  tu dhātrīṃ pītāṃ ghṛtaṃ pariṇate 'hani vāmayet tu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.43"><label>ci.17.43</label> nimbodakena madhumāgadhikāyutena
  vāntāgate 'hani ca mudgarasāśanā syāt | evaṃ tryahaṃ caturahaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ vamedvā
  sarpiḥ pibettriphalayā saha saṃyutaṃ vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.44"><label>ci.17.44</label> bhārgīṃ pibet tu payasaḥ
  pariśodhanārthamāragvadhādiṣu varaṃ madhunā kaṣāyam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.45"><label>ci.17.45</label> sāmānyametadupadiṣṭamato
  viśeṣāddoṣān payonipatitān śamayed yathāsvam | rogaṃ stanotthitamavekṣya
  bhiṣagvidadhyādyadvidradhāvabhihitaṃ bahuśo vidhānam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.46"><label>ci.17.46</label> saṃpacyamānam api taṃ tu
  vinopanāhaiḥ saṃbhojanena khalu pācayituṃ yateta | śīghraṃ stano hi
  mṛdumāṃsatayopanaddhaḥ sarvaṃ prakotham upayātyavadīryate ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.17.47"><label>ci.17.47</label> pakve tu dugdhahariṇīḥ parihṛtya
  nāḍīḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca cūcukayugaṃ vidadhīta śastram | āme vidāhini tathaiva gate ca
  pākaṃ dhātryāḥ stanau satatam eva ca nirduhīta ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
  visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ nāma saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||17 || </p>
 </div>
 <div n="18" type="adhyāya">
  <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.1"><label>ci.18.1</label> athāto
  granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.2"><label>ci.18.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3"><label>ci.18.3</label> granthiṣvathāmeṣu
  bhiṣagvidadhyācchophakriyāṃ vistaraśokāryāḥ pittārbude
  kāyavirecanaṃ ca | vighṛṣya codumbaraśākagojīpatrair bhṛśaṃ kṣaudrayutaiḥ
  pralimpet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.33"><label>ci.18.33</label> ślakṣṇīkṛtaiḥ
  sarjarasapriyaṅgupattaṅgarodhrāñjanayaṣṭikāhvaiḥ | visrāvya
  cāragvadhāgojisomāḥ śyāmā ca yojyā kuśalena lepe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.34"><label>ci.18.34</label> śyāmāgirihvāñjanakīraseṣu
  drākṣārase saptalikārase ca | ghṛtaṃ pibet klītakasaṃprasiddhaṃ pittārbudī
  tajjaṭharī ca jantuḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.35"><label>ci.18.35</label> śuddhasya jantoḥ kaphaje 'rbude tu
  rakte 'vasikte tu tato 'rbudaṃ tat | dravyāṇi yānyūrdhvamadhaś ca doṣān haranti
  taiḥ kalkakṛtaiḥ pradihyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.36"><label>ci.18.36</label> kapotapārāvataviṅvimiśraiḥ
  sakāṃsyanīlaiḥ śukalāṅgalākhyaiḥ | mūtrais tu kākādanimūlamiśraiḥ
  kṣārapradigdhair athavā pradihyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.37"><label>ci.18.37</label>
  niṣpāvapiṇyākakulatthakalkair māṃsapragāḍhair dadhimastuyuktaiḥ | lepaṃ
  vidadhyāt kṛmayo yathā 'tra mūrcchanti muñcantyatha makṣikāś ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.38"><label>ci.18.38</label> alpāvaśiṣṭe kṛmibhakṣite<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ca likhettato 'gniṃ vidadhīta
  paś cāt | yadalpamūlaṃ traputāmrasīsapaṭṭaiḥ samāveṣṭya tadāyasair vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.39"><label>ci.18.39</label> kṣārāgniśastrāṇyasakṛdvidadhyāt
  prāṇānahiṃsan bhiṣagpramattaḥ | āsphotajātīkaravīrapatraiḥ kaṣāyamiṣṭaṃ
  vraṇaśodhanārtham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.40"><label>ci.18.40</label> śuddhe ca tailaṃ vidadhīta
  bhārgīviḍaṅgapāṭhātriphalāvipakvam | yadṛcchayā copagatāni pākaṃ
  pākakrameṇopacaredvidhijñaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.41"><label>ci.18.41</label> medorbudaṃ svinnamatho vidārya
  viśodhya sīvyedgataraktamāśu | tato haridrāgṛhadhūmarodhrapataṅgacūrṇaiḥ
  samanaḥ śilālaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.42"><label>ci.18.42</label> vraṇaṃ pratigrāhya
  madhupragāḍhaiḥ karañjatailaṃ vidadhīta śuddhe | saśeṣadoṣāṇi hi yo 'rbudāni
  karoti tasyāśu punarbhavanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.43"><label>ci.18.43</label> tasmād aśeṣāṇi samuddharettu
  hanyuḥ saśeṣāṇi yathā hi vahniḥ | saṃsvedya gaṇḍaṃ pavanotthamādau
  nāḍyā 'nilaghnauṣadhapatrabhaṅgaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.44"><label>ci.18.44</label> amlaiḥ samūtrair vividhaiḥ
  payobhir uṣṇaiḥ satailaiḥ piśitaiś ca vidvān | visrāvayet svinnamatandriyaś ca
  śuddhaṃ vraṇaṃ cāpy upanāhayet tu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.45"><label>ci.18.45</label>
  śaṇātasīmūlakaśigrukiṇvapriyālamajjānuyutais tilais tu |
  kālāmṛtāśigrupunarnavārkagajādināmākarahāṭakuṣṭhaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.46"><label>ci.18.46</label> ekaiṣikāvṛkṣakatilvakaiś ca
  surāmlapiṣṭair asakṛt pradihyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.47"><label>ci.18.47</label> tailaṃ
  pibeccāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ | siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca
  sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.48"><label>ci.18.48</label> svedopanāhaiḥ kaphasaṃbhavaṃ tu
  saṃsvedaya visrāvaṇam eva kuryāt |
  tato 'jagandhātiviṣāviśalyāviṣāṇikākuṣṭhaśukāhvayābhiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.49"><label>ci.18.49</label> palāśabhasmodakapeṣitābhir dihyāt
  suguñjābhir aśītalābhiḥ | daśārdhasaṅkhyair lavaṇaiś ca yuktaṃ tailaṃ
  pibenmāgadhikādisiddham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.50"><label>ci.18.50</label> pracchardanaṃ mūrdhavirecanaṃ ca
  dhūmaś ca vair ecaniko hitas tu | pākakramo vā 'pi sadā vidheyo vaidyena
  pākaṅgatayoḥ kathañcit || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.51"><label>ci.18.51</label> kaṭutrikakṣaudrayutāḥ samūtrā
  bhakṣyā yavānnāni rasāś ca maudgāḥ | saśṛṅgaverāḥ sapaṭolanimbā hitāya deyā
  galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.52"><label>ci.18.52</label> medaḥsamutthe tu yathopadiṣṭāṃ
  vidhyet sirāṃ snigdhatanornarasya | śyāmāsudhālohapurīṣadantīrasāñjanaiś cāpi
  hitaḥ pradehaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.53"><label>ci.18.53</label> mūtreṇa vā+āloḍya hitāya sāraṃ
  prātaḥ pibet sālamahīruhāṇām | śastreṇa vā++āpāṭya vidārya cainaṃ medaḥ
  samuddhṛtya hitāya sīvyet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.54"><label>ci.18.54</label> majjājyamedomadhubhir dahedvā
  dagdhe ca sarpirmadhu cāvacāryam | kāsīsatutthe ca tato 'tra deye cūrṇīkṛte
  rocanayā samete || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.18.55"><label>ci.18.55</label> tailena cābhyajya hitāya dadyāt
  sārodbhavaṃ gomayajaṃ ca bhasma | hitaś ca nityaṃ triphalākaṣāyo gāḍhaś ca
  bandho yavabhojanaṃ ca ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
  granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||18 ||</p>
 </div>

            | kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"><label>ci.19.6</label> sakṣīraṃ vā pibenmāsaṃ tailameraṇḍasaṃbhavam
            | tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

            | vidagdhāṃ pācayitvā vā sevanīṃ parivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"><label>ci.19.9</label> bhindyāttataḥ prabhinnāyāṃ yathoktaṃ kramam
            ācaret | pittajāyāmapakvāyāṃ pittagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"><label>ci.19.10</label> pakvāṃ vā bhedayed bhinnāṃ śodhayet
            kṣaudrasarpiṣā | śuddhāyāṃ ca bhiṣagdadyāttailaṃ kalkaṃ ca ropaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"><label>ci.19.11</label> raktajāyāṃ jalaukobhiḥ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śoṇitaṃ nirharedbhiṣak | pibed virecanaṃ vā
            'pi śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"><label>ci.19.12</label> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryād āme pakve ca
            sarvadā | vṛddhiṃ kaphātmikāmuṣṇair mūtrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"><label>ci.19.13</label> pītadārukaṣāyaṃ ca piben mūtreṇa saṃyutam |
            vimlāpanād ṛte vā 'pi śleṣmagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"><label>ci.19.14</label> pakvāyāṃ ca vibhinnāyāṃ tailaṃ
            śodhanamiṣyate | sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇeṣu sādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"><label>ci.19.15</label> medaḥsamutthāṃ saṃsvedya lepayet surasādinā
            | śirovirekadravyair vā sukhoṣṇair mūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"><label>ci.19.16</label> svinnāṃ cāveṣṭya paṭṭena samāśvāsya tu
            mānavam | rakṣan phale sevanīṃ ca vṛddhipatreṇa dārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"><label>ci.19.17</label> medas tataḥ samuddhṛtya dadyāt

            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1"><label>ci.22.1</label> athāto mukharogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3"><label>ci.22.3</label> caturvidhena snehena madhūcchiṣṭayutena ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātaje 'bhyañjanaṃ  dantavaidarbhe dantamūlāni śodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ || </l>

            |

             kṛmidantakavac cāpi vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24"><label>ci.22.24</label> chittvā 'dhimāṃsaṃ sakṣaudrair ebhiścūrṇair

            <caesura/>
             paṭolatriphalānimbakaṣāyaś cātra dhāvane | hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca dhūmo vair ecanaś ca
            yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26ab"><label>ci.22.26</label> sāmānyaṃ karma nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ cātra me
            śṛṇu |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26cd"> nāḍīvraṇaharaṃ karma dantanāḍīṣu kārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27"><label>ci.22.27</label> yaṃ dantam abhijāyeta nāḍī taṃ dantamuddharet |
            <caesura/>
             chittvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28"><label>ci.22.28</label> śodhayitvā dahec cāpi kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā
            |
            <caesura/>
             bhinattyupekṣite dante hanukāsthi gatirdhruvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29"><label>ci.22.29</label> samūlaṃ daśanaṃ tasmād
            uddharedbhagnamasthiram |
            <caesura/>
             uddhṛte tūttare dante  ca sthānaṃ vidahet suṣirasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             tato vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41"><label>ci.22.41</label> tailaṃ daśaguṇe kṣīre siddhaṃ nasye hitaṃ
            bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             hanomokṣe samuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāc cārditavat kriyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.42"><label>ci.22.42</label> phalānyamlāni śītāmbu rūkṣānnaṃ
            dantadhāvanam |
            <caesura/>
             tathā 'tikaṭhinān bhakṣyān dantarogī vivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.43"><label>ci.22.43</label> sādhyānāṃ dantarogāṇāṃ cikitsitamudīritam |
            <caesura/>
             jihvāgatānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma vakṣyāmi siddhaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.44"><label>ci.22.44</label> auṣṭhaprakope 'nilaje yaduktaṃ prāk
            cikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭakeṣv anilottheṣu tat kāryaṃ bhiṣajā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.45"><label>ci.22.45</label> pittajeṣu vighṛṣṭeṣu niḥsṛte duṣṭaśoṇite |
            <caesura/>
             pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣaṃ nasyaṃ ca madhuraṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.46"><label>ci.22.46</label> kaṇṭakeṣu kaphottheṣu likhiteṣv asṛjaḥ
            kṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             pippalyādirmadhuyutaḥ kāryas tu pratisāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.47"><label>ci.22.47</label> gṛhṇīyāt kavalāṃś cāpi
            gaurasarṣapasaindhavaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolanimbavārtākukṣārayūṣaiś ca bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.48"><label>ci.22.48</label> upajihvāṃ tu saṃlikhya kṣāreṇa pratisārayet
            |
            <caesura/>
             śirovirekagaṇḍūṣadhūmaiś cainamupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.49"><label>ci.22.49</label> jihvāgatānāṃ karmoktaṃ tālavyānāṃ
            pravakṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             aṅguṣṭhāṅgulisaṃdaṃśenākṛṣya galaśuṇḍikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50ab"><label>ci.22.50</label> chedayen maṇḍalāgreṇa jihvopari tu
            saṃsthitām |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50cd"> notkṛṣṭaṃ caiva hīnaṃ ca tribhāgaṃ chedayed bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.51"><label>ci.22.51</label> atyādānāt sravedraktaṃ tannimittaṃ mriyeta
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             hīnacchedādbhavecchopho lālā nidrā bhramastamaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.52"><label>ci.22.52</label> tasmād vaidyaḥ prayatnena dṛṣṭakarmā
            viśāradaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             galaśuṇḍīṃ tu sañchidya kuryāt prāptamimaṃ kramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.53"><label>ci.22.53</label> maricātiviṣāpāṭhāvacākuṣṭhakuṭannaṭaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudrayuktaiḥ salavaṇais tatastāṃ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.54"><label>ci.22.54</label> vacāmativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ rāsnāṃ kaṭukarohiṇīm |
            <caesura/>
             niṣkvāthya picumandaṃ ca kavalaṃ tatra yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.55"><label>ci.22.55</label> iṅgudīkiṇihīdantīsaralāsuradārubhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pañcāṅgīṃ kārayet piṣṭair vartiṃ gandhottarāṃ śubhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.56"><label>ci.22.56</label> tato dhūmaṃ pibejjanturdvirahnaḥ
            kaphanāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārasiddheṣu mudgeṣu yūṣaś cāpyaśane hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.57"><label>ci.22.57</label> tuṇḍikeryadhruṣe kūrme saṅghāte tālupuppuṭe
            |
            <caesura/>
             eṣa eva vidhiḥ kāryo viśeṣaḥ śastrakarmaṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.58"><label>ci.22.58</label> tālupāke tu kartavyaṃ vidhānaṃ pittanāśanam
            |
            <caesura/>
             snehasvedau tāluśoṣe vidhiś cānilanāśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.59"><label>ci.22.59</label> kīrtitaṃ tālujānāṃ tu kaṇṭhyānāṃ karma
            vakṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             sādhyānāṃ rohiṇīnāṃ tu hitaṃ śoṇitamokṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.60"><label>ci.22.60</label> chardanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca gaṇḍūṣo nasyakarma
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātikīṃ tu hṛte rakte lavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.61"><label>ci.22.61</label> sukhoṣṇān snehagaṇḍūṣān
            dhārayeccāpyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pataṅgaśarkarākṣaudraiḥ paittikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.62"><label>ci.22.62</label> drākṣāparūṣakakvātho hitaś ca kavalagrahe |
            <caesura/>
             agāradhūmakaṭukaiḥ ślaiṣmikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.63"><label>ci.22.63</label> śvetāviḍaṅgadantīṣu tailaṃ siddhaṃ
            sasaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             nasyakarmaṇi yoktavyaṃ tathā kavaladhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.64"><label>ci.22.64</label> pittavat sādhayed vaidyo rohiṇīṃ
            raktasaṃbhavām |
            <caesura/>
             visrāvya kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ sādhayettuṇḍikerivat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.65"><label>ci.22.65</label> ekakālaṃ yavānnaṃ ca bhuñjīta
            snigdhamalpaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             upajihvikavac cāpi sādhayed adhijihvikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.66"><label>ci.22.66</label> ekavṛndaṃ tu visrāvya vidhiṃ śodhanamācaret
            |
            <caesura/>
             gilāyuś cāpi yo vyādhistaṃ ca śastreṇa sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.67"><label>ci.22.67</label> amarmasthaṃ supakvaṃ ca bhedayed
            galavidradhim |
            <caesura/>
             vātāt sarvasaraṃ cūrṇair lavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.68"><label>ci.22.68</label> tailaṃ vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ
            kavalanasyayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tato 'smai snaihikaṃ dhūmamimaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.69"><label>ci.22.69</label> śālarājādanair aṇḍasāraiṅgudamadhūkajāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             majjāno gugguludhyāmamāṃsīkālānusārivāḥ | śrīsarjarasaśaileyamadhūcchiṣṭāni cāharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.70"><label>ci.22.70</label> tat sarvaṃ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ snehenāloḍya
            yuktitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ṭiṇḍūkavṛntaṃ sakṣaudraṃ matimāṃstena lepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.71"><label>ci.22.71</label> eṣa sarvasare dhūmaḥ praśastaḥ snaihiko
            mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaphaghno mārutaghnaś ca mukharogavināśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.72"><label>ci.22.72</label> pittātmake sarvasare śuddhakāyasya dehinaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.73"><label>ci.22.73</label> pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣau dhūmaḥ saṃśodhanāni ca
            |
            <caesura/>
             kaphātmake sarvasare vidhiṃ kuryāt kaphāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.74"><label>ci.22.74</label> pibedativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ mustaṃ ca suradāru ca
            | rohiṇīṃ kaṭukākhyāṃ ca kuṭajasya phalāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.75"><label>ci.22.75</label> gavāṃ mūtreṇa manujo bhāgair
            dharaṇasaṃmitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṣa sarvān kaphakṛtān rogān yogo 'pakarṣati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.76"><label>ci.22.76</label> kṣīrekṣurasagomūtradadhimastvamlakāñjikaiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             vidadhyāt kavalān vīkṣya doṣaṃ tailaghṛtair api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.77"><label>ci.22.77</label> rogāṇāṃ mukhajātānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma
            kīrtitam |
            <caesura/>
             asādhyā api vakṣyante rogā ye tatra kīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.78"><label>ci.22.78</label> auṣṭhaprakope varjyāḥ syur
            māṃsaraktatridoṣajāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dantamūleṣu varjyau tu triliṅgagatisauṣirau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.79"><label>ci.22.79</label> danteṣu ca na sidhyanti
            śyāvadālanabhañjanāḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.80"><label>ci.22.80</label> svaraghno valayo vṛndo vidāryalasa eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             galauṣṭho māṃsatānaś ca śataghnī rohiṇī ca yā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.81"><label>ci.22.81</label> asādhyāḥ kīrtitā hyete rogā nava daśaiva ca
            |
            <caesura/>
             teṣāṃ cāpi kriyāṃ vaidyaḥ pratyākhyāya samācaret ||</l>

            'dhyāyaḥ ||22 ||</p>

        <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
          <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.1"><label>ci.24.1</label> athāto 'nāgatābādhāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.2"><label>ci.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.3"><label>ci.24.3</label> utthāyotthāya satataṃ svasthenārogyam icchatā
            |
            <caesura/>
             dhīmatā yad anuṣṭheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.4"><label>ci.24.4</label> tatrādau dantapavanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulamāyatam |
            <caesura/>
             kaniṣṭhikāparīṇāham ṛjvagranthitam avraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.5"><label>ci.24.5</label> ayugmagranthi yac cāpi pratyagraṃ
            śastabhūmijam |
            <caesura/>
             avekṣyartuṃ ca doṣaṃ ca rasaṃ vīryaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.6"><label>ci.24.6</label> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukaṃ prātar
            utthitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nimbaś ca tiktake śreṣṭhaḥ kaṣāye khadiras tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.7"><label>ci.24.7</label> madhūko madhure śreṣṭhaḥ karañjaḥ kaṭuke
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudravyoṣatrivargāktaṃ satailaṃ saindhavena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.8"><label>ci.24.8</label> cūrṇena tejovatyāś ca dantān nityaṃ
            viśodhayet | ekaikaṃ ghrṣayed dantaṃ mṛdunā kūrcakena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.9"><label>ci.24.9</label> dantaśodhanacūrṇena dantamāṃsāny abādhayan |
            <caesura/>
             tad daurgandhyopadehau tu śleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.10"><label>ci.24.10</label> vaiśadyam annābhir uciṃ saumanasyaṃ karoti
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             na khāded galatālv oṣṭhajihvārogasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.11"><label>ci.24.11</label> athāsyapāke śvāse ca kāsahikkāvamīṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaś ca mūrcchārto madapīṣitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.12"><label>ci.24.12</label> śirorujārtastṛṣitaḥ śrāntaḥ pānaklamānvitaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             arditī karṇaśūlī ca dantarogī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.13"><label>ci.24.13</label> jihvānirlekhanaṃ raupyaṃ sauvarṇaṃ vārkṣam
            eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             tan malāpaharaṃ śastaṃ mṛdu ślakṣṇaṃ daśāṅgulam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.14"><label>ci.24.14</label> mukhavair asya daurgandhyaśophajāḍyaharaṃ
            sukham |
            <caesura/>
             dantadārḍhyakaraṃ rucyaṃ snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.15"><label>ci.24.15</label> kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyair vā kṣīreṇa ca
            vimiśritaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhilloṭakakaṣāyeṇa tathaivāmalakasya vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.16"><label>ci.24.16</label> prakṣālayen mukhaṃ nentre svasthaḥ
            śītodakena vā |
            <caesura/>
             nīlikāṃ mukhaśoṣaṃ ca piḍakāṃ vyaṅgam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.17"><label>ci.24.17</label> raktapittakṛtān rogān sadya eva vināśayet |
            <caesura/>
             sukhaṃ laghu nirīkṣeta dṛḍhaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.18"><label>ci.24.18</label> mataṃ srotoñjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ viśuddhaṃ

            svapnajāgaraṇaśayanāsanasthānacaṅkramaṇayānavāhanapradhāvanalaṅghanaplavanaprataraṇahāsyabhāṣyavyavāyavyāyāmādīnucitān
            apy atiseveta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.97"><label>ci.24.97</label> ucitād apy ahitāt kramaśo viramet, hitam
            anucitam apy aseveta kramaśaḥ, na caikāntataḥ pādahīnāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.98"><label>ci.24.98</label> nāvākśirāḥ śayīta, na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta,
            na vinā pātreṇa, nāñjalipuṭenāpaḥ pibet, kāle hitamitasnigdhamadhuraprāyamāhāraṃ
            vaidyapratyavekṣitam aśnīyāt, grāmagaṇagaṇikāpaṇikaśatrusatraśaṭhapatitabhojanāni
            parikaret, śeṣāṇy api cāniṣṭarūparasagandhasparśaśabdamānasāni, anyāny evaṃ guṇāny api
            saṃbhramadattāni, (tānyapi) makṣikābālopahatāni, nāprakṣālitapādo bhuñjīta na
            mūtroccārapīḍito na sandhyayor nānupāśrito nātītakālaṃ hīnam atimātraṃ (noddhṛtasnehaṃ)
            ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"><label>ci.24.99</label> na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ naṣṭaṃ paryuṣitaṃ
            payaḥ | na naktaṃ dadhi bhuñjīta na cāpy aghṛtaśarkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"><label>ci.24.100</label> nāmudgayūṣaṃ nākṣaudraṃ noṣṇaṃ nāmalakair
            vinā | anyathā janayet kuṣṭhavisarpādīn gadān bahūn | nātmānamudake paśyen na nagnaḥ
            praviśejjalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101"><label>ci.24.101</label>
            dyūtamadyātisevāpratibhutvasākṣitvasamāhvānagoṣṭhīvāditrāṇi na seveta, srajaṃ
            chatropānakau kanakam atītavāsāṃsi na cānyair dhṛtāni dhārayet, brāhmaṇam agniṃ gāṃ ca
            nocchiṣṭaḥ spṛśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102"><label>ci.24.102</label> bhavanti cātra yasmin yasminn ṛtau ye ye
            doṣāḥ kupyanti dehinām |
            <caesura/>
             teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasāste te vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103"><label>ci.24.103</label> varṣāsu na pibet toyaṃ pibec charadi
            mātrayā |
            <caesura/>
             varṣasu caturo māsān mātrāvad udakaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104"><label>ci.24.104</label> uṣṇaṃ haime vasante ca kāmaṃ śrīṣme tu

            <caesura/>
             hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105"><label>ci.24.105</label> śṛtaśītaṃ payo grīṣme prāvṛṭkāle rasaṃ
            pibet |
            <caesura/>
             yūṣaṃ varṣati, tasyānte prapicchītalaṃ jalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106"><label>ci.24.106</label> svastha evam ato 'nyas tu
            doṣāhāragatānugaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snehaṃ saindhavacūrṇena pippalībhiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107"><label>ci.24.107</label> pibed agnivivṛddhyarthaṃ na ca vegān

            <caesura/>
             agnidīptikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ rogāṇāṃ śamanaṃ prati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108"><label>ci.24.108</label> prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu samyak
            snehādimācaret |
            <caesura/>
             kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte vireko bastirīrane || </l>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
             tribhis tribhir ahobhir vā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"><label>ci.24.114</label> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt pakṣād
            vrajed budhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rajasvalām akāmāṃ ca malinām apriyāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"><label>ci.24.115</label> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label>ci.24.122</label> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hānir adharmaś ca tato
            bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrām atha parvasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label>ci.24.123</label> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoś cāpi gacchato
            jīvitakṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label>ci.24.124</label> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ
            vandhyāmasaṃvṛte |
            <caesura/>
             deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label>ci.24.125</label> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaś ca madhyāhne
            tṛṣito 'balaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>ci.24.126</label> atiprasaṅgād bhavati śoṣaḥ
            śukrakṣayāvahaḥ | vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyur mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>ci.24.127</label> prayūṣasy ardharātre ca vātapitte
            prakupyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tiryagyonāv ayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>ci.24.128</label> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ śukrasya ca
            kṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>ci.24.129</label> uttāne ca bhavec chīghraṃ śukrāśmaryās tu
            saṃbhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaṃ pariharet tasmād etal lokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>ci.24.130</label> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna sandhāryaṃ
            kathaṃcana |
            <caesura/>
             vayor ūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>ci.24.131</label> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām
            alaṅkṛtām |
            <caesura/>
             seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>ci.24.132</label> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ sasitaṃ rasa
            eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>ci.24.133</label> mukhamātraṃ samāsena sadvṛttasyaitad
            īritam |
            <caesura/>
             ārogyam āyur artho vāg āsadbhiḥ prāpyate nṛbhiḥ ||</l>

            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhogrā syāt surāṣṭrodbhavā ca pattaṅgaṃ vai rocanā cāñjanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"><label>ci.25.39</label> hemāṅgatvak pāṇḍupatraṃ vaṭasya kālīyaṃ
            syāt padmakaṃ padmamadhyam |
            <caesura/>
             raktaṃ śvetaṃ candanaṃ pāradaṃ ca kākolyādiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaś ca vargaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40"><label>ci.25.40</label> medo majjā sikthakaṃ goghṛtaṃ ca dugdhaṃ
            kvāthaḥ kṣīriṇāṃ ca drumāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             etat sarvaṃ pakvam aikadhyatas tu vaktrābhyaṅge sarpir uktaṃ pradhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41"><label>ci.25.41</label> hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ cātivṛddhāṃ vaktre
            jātāḥ sphoṭikāś cāpi kāścit |
            <caesura/>
             padmākāraṃ nirvalīkaṃ ca vaktraṃ kuryād etat pīnagaṇḍaṃ manojñam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42"><label>ci.25.42</label> rājñām etad yoṣitāṃ cāpi nityaṃ kuryād
            vaidyas tat samānāṃ nṛṇāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaghnaṃ vai sarpiretat pradhānaṃ yeṣāṃ pāde santi vaipādikāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.43"><label>ci.25.43</label> harīkakīcūrṇamariṣṭapatraṃ cūtatvacaṃ
            dāḍimapuṣpavṛntam |
            <caesura/>
             patraṃ ca dadyān madayantikāyā lepo 'ṅgarāgo naradevayogyaḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne miśrakacikitsitaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||25 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="26" type="adhyāya">

          <head>ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>ci.26.1</label> athātaḥ kṣīṇabalīyaṃ vājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"><label>ci.26.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"><label>ci.26.3</label> kalyasyodagravayaso vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarveṣv ṛtuṣv ahar ahar vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"><label>ci.26.4</label> sthavirāṇāṃ riraṃsūnāṃ strīṇāṃ vāllabhyam
            icchatām |
            <caesura/>
             yoṣitprasaṅgāt kṣīṇānāṃ klībānām alparetasām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"><label>ci.26.5</label> vilāsinām arthavatāṃ rūpayauvanaśālinām |
            <caesura/>
             nṛṇāṃ ca bahubhāryāṇāṃ yogā vājīkarā hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"><label>ci.26.6</label> sevamāno yad aucityād vājīvāty arthavegavān |
            <caesura/>
             nārīs tarpayate tena vājīkaraṇam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>ci.26.7</label> bhojanāni vicitrāṇi pānāni vividhāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             vācaḥ śrotrānugāminyas tvacaḥ sparśasukhās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"><label>ci.26.8</label> yāminī sendutilakā kāminī navayauvanā |
            <caesura/>
             gītaṃ śrotramanohāri tāmbūlaṃ madirāḥ srajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"><label>ci.26.9</label> gandhā manojñā rūpāṇi citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             manasaś cāpratīghāto vājīkurvanti mānavam |
            <caesura/>
             tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>ci.26.10</label> dveṣyastrīsaṃprayogāc ca klaibyaṃ tan
            mānasaṃ smṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭukāmloṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>ci.26.11</label> saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaibyaṃ tad aparaṃ
            smṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             ativyavāyaśīlo yo na ca vājīkriyārataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"><label>ci.26.12</label> dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti
            tacchukrakṣayahetukam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"><label>ci.26.13</label> klaibyam etac caturthaṃ syān nṝṇāṃ

        <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"><label>ci.28.1</label> athāto medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ<ref
              rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"><label>ci.28.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"><label>ci.28.3</label> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ
            śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya
            snehakumbhe saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau nidadhyāt, saptarātrāduddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya
            yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacched anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet;
            bhallātakavidhānavaccāgārapraveśaḥ, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe himābhir adbhiḥ
            pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca payasā śarkarāmadhureṇaudanamaśnīyāt; evaṃ
            ṣaṇmāsānupayujya vigatapāpmā balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur
            bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ pāṇḍurogiṇamudariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā gormūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ
            vigatalauhitye savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam
            aśnīyāt, evaṃ māsam upayujya smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati |
            eṣaevopayogaścitrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś ca; citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ paraṃ
            pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"><label>ci.28.4</label> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
            yathākramamāgāraṃ praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ yavānnaṃ
            payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayettrīn māsān payo 'nupānaṃ, jīrṇe payaḥ
            sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī śrutanigādī bhavati
            varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātramenāṃ bhakṣayet, trirātrādūrdhvaṃ
            payaḥ sarpiriti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ piṇḍaṃ vā payasā++āloḍya pibet, evaṃ
            dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"><label>ci.28.5</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalampayuñjīta, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet, kṣīrasātmyo vā payasā
            bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī medhāvī bhavati, dvitīyaṃ saptarātram
            upayujya granthamīpsitamutpādayati naṣṭaṃ cāsya prādurbhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram
            upayujya dviruccāritaṃ śatamapyavadhārayati, evam ekaviṃśatirātram
            upayujyālakṣmīrapakrāmati; mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevyanupraviśati, sarvāś cainaṃ śrutaya
            upatiṣṭhanti, śrutadharaḥ pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"><label>ci.28.6</label> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprasthaṃ
            viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayor dvādaśa harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni
            ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tataḥ pūrvavidhānena
            mātrāṃ yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, pūrvavaccātra
            parīhāraḥ, etenordhvamadhastiryak kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīrapakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ
            sthiravayāḥ śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyurbhavati; etad eva
            kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu saṃśodhanamādiśanti
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"><label>ci.28.7</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ
            piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ,
            evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ vivriyate, dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān
            bhavati, trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte, caturdvādaśarātram upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ,
            tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate, śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya
            pibet payasā, samānaṃ bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"><label>ci.28.8</label> vacāśatapākaṃ vā sarpirdroṇam upayujya
            pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati, galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃś cāpahantīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"><label>ci.28.9</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi āyuṣkāmarasāyanam |
            mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"><label>ci.28.10</label> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ vārān
            sahasraśaḥ | śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"><label>ci.28.11</label> sarpirmdhuyutaṃ lihyādalakṣmīnāśanaṃ param
            | tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"><label>ci.28.12</label> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā hutvā
            samāhitaḥ | daśasāhassramāyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"><label>ci.28.13</label> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu madhulājaiś ca
            saṃyutam | amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"><label>ci.28.14</label> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ
            priyaṅgavaḥ | gavyena payasā pītamalakṣmīṃ pratibedhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"><label>ci.28.15</label> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena payasā śṛtaḥ |
            sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdhamalakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"><label>ci.28.16</label> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca
            mākṣikam | pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"><label>ci.28.17</label> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca bilvacūrṇam iti trayam
            | medhyamāyuṣyamārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"><label>ci.28.18</label> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailamāvāpya sādhitam |
            hutvā sahasramaśnīyānmedhyamāyuṣyamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"><label>ci.28.19</label> yāvakāṃstāvakān khādedabhibhūya yavāṃs
            tathā | pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavadbhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"><label>ci.28.20</label> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇam iti ca trayam
            | prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"><label>ci.28.21</label> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyagupayuktaṃ dine dine |
            sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayed vaśe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"><label>ci.28.22</label> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ mākṣikaṃ madhu
            | suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyamicchatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"><label>ci.28.23</label> padmanīlotpalakvāthe yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute |
            sarpirāsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā paibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"><label>ci.28.24</label> payaś cānupibet siddhaṃ teṣām eva
            samudbhave | alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā++āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"><label>ci.28.25</label> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣveteṣu sādhane |
            śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"><label>ci.28.26</label> pāpmānaṃ nāśayantyetā dadyuś cauṣadhayaḥ
            śriyam | kuryurnāgabalaṃ cāpi manuṣyamamaropamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"><label>ci.28.27</label> satatādhyayanaṃ vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanam |
            tadvidyācāryasevā ca buddhimedhākaro guṇaḥ(gaṇaḥ) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"><label>ci.28.28</label> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ cāvidhāraṇam
            | brahmacaryamahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"><label>ci.29.1</label> athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"><label>ci.29.7</label> gāyatrastraiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ śākvaras
